#### 7.4.5.9.2 Raw power calculation

#### 7.4.5.9.3 Interference and noise power estimation

##### 7.4.5.9.3.1 Noise power estimation algorithm

###### 7.4.5.9.3.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.9.3.1.1.0-3**  (ID: `11412794`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL(RU) shall support the new R&D parameter **rdDmrsPowerType2ThrPusch (see 5G\_L1\_17496\_replaced([11412788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e98d9_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

Once abs(s)^2 <= rdDmrsPowerType2ThrPusch on one DMRS RE, normalized raw CE and 1/abs(s)^2 on this RE shall be replaced by the closest DMRS RE with abs(s)^2 >rdDmrsPowerType2ThrPusch.​

Once the number of DMRE RE with abs(s)^2 <= rdDmrsPowerType2ThrPusch is more than or equal to half of total DMRS RE, noise power shall be estimated only on these DMRS REs by its power.​ (for more detail 5G\_L1\_17496\_replaced([11412788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e98d9_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

###### 7.4.5.9.3.1.2 Odin

###### 7.4.5.9.3.1.2.0-1 Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin 12649280: Odin Noise power estimation is performed in CE MDAB. It is based on raw channel estimation after layer separation. Layer separation is described in section "2.3.1.2 Layer separation" of 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G_L1_2794). Total interference plus noise power estimation (NPE) algorithm is described in section "2.3.1.4 Noise power estimation" of 5GMax algorithm specification. This algorithm provides noise estimation per receiving antenna and layer. The noise is estimated on the used resource elements of the first DMRS symbol. Simplification of the noise power estimation algorithm for PUSCH is introduced by substituting weighting Matrix S with alternative matrix M. Matrix M is derived from LDL decomposition of S, i.e., [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in dark text on a white background. The equation is: S = V · E · VH = (VE1/2) · (VE1/2)H = MMH The equation appears to be related to matrix operations, where 'V' and 'E' are likely matrices, and 'H' denotes the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose). 'S' and 'M' are also likely matrices. The term E1/2 suggests a matrix square root.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2298.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Matrix M is precomputed and stored in memory. No performance loss expected and, due to M having reduced column dimension, less DSP operations are required. The simplified noise power estimate (per chunk block i, antenna port p and spatial stream ant)  is: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $\hat{\sigma} {noise,i,p,ant}^2 = (\hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot})^H MM^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot} = (M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot})^H (M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot}) = \sum {k=1}^{R} |[M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}] {k}|^2$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2298.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] Full description of the simplification and notation in section "2.3.1.4" of 5Gmax algorithm specification (5G_L1_7703_replaced( 11396538 )). (ID: 12649280)

The letters are large and appear to be in a sans-serif typeface. The "N" is on the left, followed by "PRE" to its right. The letters have a slight chromatic aberration, giving them a subtle rainbow effect, particularly around the edges. The background is white, and the text is dark, possibly black or a very dark gray. The image is cropped closely to the text, with a thin black border around the entire image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2303.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]  is parameter numOfPrb of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Power estimation compensation is described in section "2.3.1.5 Noise Power Compensation" of "5GMax algorithm specification".

When the DMRS ports are in the same CDM group, the noise power estimation is completed by an estimation of the interference on the unused resource elements.

This is described in section "2.3.5 Interference Power Estimation" of "5GMax algorithm specification".

##### 7.4.5.9.3.3 Noise power estimation for MU-MIMO receiver

###### 7.4.5.9.3.3.1 Thor

**7.4.5.9.3.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11412834`)

Thor
For [CB010708-G-UPD001] C16'2 [End CB010708-G-UPD001], C16'4 and [CB008235-A] C16'8 [End CB008235-A] subcell type and in case of MU-MIMO receiver, the contribution of unused REs to noise power estimation shall be restricted to the own antennas/spatial streams of each paired UE. 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall set to 0 the NPE computation results based on unused DMRS REs of Rx antennas/spatial streams that are allocated to other UEs of the same pairing group.

As a consequence, the computation of noisePower, linNoiseOfAnt and sinrOfAnt  in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs is impacted.

The requirement is valid for up to [Before CB008235-A] 4 [CB008235-A] 8 [End CB008235-A] paired UEs per PRB.

For C16'2 and C16'4 subcell type and in case of MU-MIMO receiver, the contribution of unused REs to noise power estimation shall be restricted to the own antennas/spatial streams of each paired UE. 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall set to 0 the NPE computation results based on unused DMRS REs of Rx antennas/spatial streams that are allocated to other UEs of the same pairing group.

As a consequence, the computation of *noisePower,* linNoiseOfAnt and *sinrOfAnt  in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs is impacted.\*\*\*\*

The requirement is valid for up to 4 paired UEs per PRB.

#### 7.4.5.9.4 Unused RE noise power estimation &gt; Refer to "Interference and Noise Power Estimation"

#### 7.4.5.9.5 Timing offset estimation and compensation

##### 7.4.5.9.5.1 Thor

**7.4.5.9.5.1.0-3**  (ID: `11412862`)

Thor
Timing offset estimation

Timing offset (TO) estimation is performed in CE MDAB, based on channel estimates. It requires the conversion of the frequency-domain estimated channel response to time domain by using IFFT. IFFT size for TO estimation (TOE) is constrained to 64, 128 and 256, according to the number of DMRS RE. When DMRS RE number exceeds 256, only the first 256 raw channel estimates are selected to perform TO estimation.

If DMRS RE number <= 64

IFFT size = 64

Elseif DMRS RE number <= 128

IFFT size = 128

Else

IFFT size = 256

End

The number of PUSCH DMRS RE is derived from parameters numOfPrb and ulDmrsConfigType in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For ulDmrsConfigType 1, the calculation is numDmrsRe = ceil (numOfPrb/2) \* 12.

A ratio is defined to reflect the IFFT size impact, and shall be used to derive an equivalent CP length and a final TO estimate.

The search window length for time offset estimation is 2/3 CP length, and the search window range is symmetric.

[CB008235-B] TOE shall be supported for TD-PDP or mixture PDP algorithm for PDP length determination as described in 5G\_L1\_18576\_replaced([11412929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99sEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008235-B]

The timing offset estimation algorithm for PUSCH is described in section "2.3.4.1 TO Estimation in Time Domain" of "5GMax algorithm specification"(see 5G\_L1\_2794).

---

##### 7.4.5.9.5.2 Odin

**7.4.5.9.5.2.0-2**  (ID: `12649431`)

Odin
Timing offset estimation

Timing offset (TO) estimation is performed in CE MDAB, based on channel estimates. It requires the conversion of the frequency-domain estimated channel response to time domain by using IFFT. IFFT size for TO estimation (TOE) is constrained to 64, 128 and 256, according to the number of DMRS RE. When DMRS RE number exceeds 256, only the first 256 raw channel estimates are selected to perform TO estimation.

If DMRS RE number <= 64

IFFT size = 64

Elseif DMRS RE number <= 128

IFFT size = 128

Else

IFFT size = 256

End

The number of PUSCH DMRS RE is derived from parameters numOfPrb and ulDmrsConfigType in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For ulDmrsConfigType 1, the calculation is numDmrsRe = ceil (numOfPrb/2) \* 12.

A ratio is defined to reflect the IFFT size impact, and shall be used to derive an equivalent CP length and a final TO estimate.

The search window length for time offset estimation is 2/3 CP length, and the search window range is symmetric.

The timing offset estimation algorithm for PUSCH is described in section "2.3.4.1 TO Estimation in Time Domain" of "5GMax algorithm specification"(see 5G\_L1\_2794).

---

#### 7.4.5.9.6 Power delay profile determination

##### 7.4.5.9.6.0-1 Power delay profile determination Start from 5GC001981-A, adaptive per RX PDP (Power Delay Profile) length determination is supported for PUSCH, as described in section "2.3.4.4 Adaptive PDP length determination" of 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document (5G_L1_2794). The simulation report is available at " Performance comparison between combined and per Rx smoother indicator.pptx " (ID: 11412873)

#### 7.4.5.9.7 DTX detection

### 7.4.5.10 Channel estimation post-processing - SxC domain

#### 7.4.5.10.1 SNR estimation

#### 7.4.5.10.2 MMSE smoother selection

#### 7.4.5.10.3 MMSE smoothing

#### 7.4.5.10.4 PDP length determination and MMSE smoothing

##### 7.4.5.10.4.1 Thor

**7.4.5.10.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11412941`)

Thor
L1-RU shall support channel estimation smoothing, as described in section **[Before CB008235-B] "2.3.1.3 MMSE smoothing"** [CB008235-B] "#sec-PuschMmseSmoooth" **[End CB008235-B] of "5GMax algorithm specification".**\*\*\*\*

Adaptive channel estimation smoother filter length is supported. It depends on SNR and power delay profile (PDP) length **[CB008235-B] determined by time domain PDP (TD-PDP) or mixture PDP method** [End CB008235-B].\*\*\*\*

PDP length (short, mid or long) is decided after TO estimation by :

a. Defining several additional sub sections within the CP length

b. Comparing signal power to noise power among different CP sub sections

Details are given in section "2.3.4.4 Adaptive PDP length determination" of "5GMax Algorithm Specification"**[CB008235-B] for TD-PDP method and section "2.3.1.4 Adaptive Frequency Domain PDP length determination" for frequency domain PDP (FD-PDP) method** [End CB008235-B] .\*\*\*\*

[Before PR825660]  
[CB008235-B]

When RU subcell type C16\_8 is configured and R&D parameter rdUlTdFdPDPMixture (5G\_L1\_18582\_replaced(11414200)) is enabled, L1-RU shall support mixture PDP method and shall compute PDP length per UE grant:

a. using TD-PDP algorithm for UE's own beam(s)

b. using FD-PDP algorithm for other beam(s)

Otherwise, L1-RU shall always compute PDP length per spatial stream via TD-PDP method.

Note:

a. rdUlTdFdPDPMixture shall be ignored by L1-RU in case of RU subcell type is not C16\_8.

b. The PDP length indicator for each spatial stream per UE is only estimated on the first layer but applied for all layers if exist. This helps to reduce complexity.

c. For SU MIMO, it is always TD-PDP method used as all beams belong to the same UE.

[End CB008235-B]

[PR825660]

If RU subcell type is C16\_8,  at least one Virtual UE has double DMRS and rdUlTdFdPDPMixture is enabled, all of vUEs e.g vUE(a) & vUE(b) in this slot shall be applied with mixture-PDP.

[End PR825660]

---

##### 7.4.5.10.4.2 Odin

**7.4.5.10.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `12649448`)

Odin
L1-RU shall support channel estimation smoothing, as described in section "2.3.1.3 MMSE smoothing" of "5GMax algorithm specification".

Adaptive channel estimation smoother filter length is supported. It depends on SNR and power delay profile (PDP) length.

PDP length (short, mid or long) is decided after TO estimation by :

a. Defining several additional sub sections within the CP length

b. Comparing signal power to noise power among different CP sub sections

Details are given in section "2.3.4.4 Adaptive PDP length determination" of "5GMax Algorithm Specification".

### 7.4.5.12 FOE &amp; PNE

#### 7.4.5.12.1 Frequency Offset Estimation

##### 7.4.5.12.1.1 FOE input parameters and selection

###### 7.4.5.12.1.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.12.1.1.1.0-4**  (ID: `12706370`)

Thor
(Since 26R1) Carrier Frequency Offset (CFO) estimation and compensation shall be performed on PUSCH on Thor-RU.

Upon reception of the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message provided by L2-PS via L1-BB, L1-RU shall get beam-wise long-term CFO estimate using the metric* longTermCfoMetricOfBeam *contained in this message. The estimate shall be then used to compensate the CFO on the received PUSCH signal on the appropriate spatial streams (expected at the SFN and NR-slot specified in the same* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message).\*\*\*\*

The relationship between the elements of  *longTermCfoMetricOfBeam, beams* and spatial streams is given in the table below.\*\*

**[Before CB008235-SR-X]**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | LT FOE for antenna j | Beam ID | (e)CPRI spatial streams | First supporting feature |
| C4’2 | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | patternId[0] | stream 0 | CB007595-B |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | patternId[0] | stream 1 |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | patternId[1] | stream 2 |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | patternId[1] | stream 3 |  |  |
| C16’2 C16’4 C16'8 | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | patternId[0] | streams *startAntIndex &* startAndIndex+1\*\* | CB010708-A |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | patternId[1] | streams *startAntIndex+2 &* startAndIndex+3\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | patternId[2] | streams *startAntIndex+4 &* startAndIndex+5\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | patternId[3] | streams *startAntIndex+6 &* startAndIndex+7\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[4] | patternId[4] | streams *startAntIndex+8 &* startAndIndex+9\*\* | CB010708-D |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[5] | patternId[5] | streams *startAntIndex+10 &* startAndIndex+11\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[6] | patternId[6] | streams *startAntIndex+12 &* startAndIndex+13\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[7] | patternId[7] | streams *startAntIndex+14 &* startAndIndex+15\*\* |  |  |

**[CB008235-SR-X]**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | LT FOE for antenna j | Beam ID | (e)CPRI spatial streams | First supporting feature |
| ~~C4’2~~ | ~~longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]~~ | ~~patternId[0]~~ | ~~stream 0~~ | ~~CB007595-B~~ |
| ~~longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]~~ | ~~patternId[0]~~ | ~~stream 1~~ |  |  |
| ~~longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]~~ | ~~patternId[1]~~ | ~~stream 2~~ |  |  |
| ~~longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]~~ | ~~patternId[1]~~ | ~~stream 3~~ |  |  |
| C16’2 C16’4 C16'8 | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | patternId[0] | streams *startAntIndex &* startAndIndex+1\*\* | CB010708-A |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | patternId[1] | streams *startAntIndex+2 &* startAndIndex+3\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | patternId[2] | streams *startAntIndex+4 &* startAndIndex+5\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | patternId[3] | streams *startAntIndex+6 &* startAndIndex+7\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[4] | patternId[4] | streams *startAntIndex+8 &* startAndIndex+9\*\* | CB010708-D |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[5] | patternId[5] | streams *startAntIndex+10 &* startAndIndex+11\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[6] | patternId[6] | streams *startAntIndex+12 &* startAndIndex+13\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[7] | patternId[7] | streams *startAntIndex+14 &* startAndIndex+15\*\* |  |  |

**[End CB008235-SR-X]**

L2-PS provides beam-wise LT-CFO metrics only for the allocated beams of the UE. CFO estimation shall be performed only on the owned streams of the UE, determined by parameters *startAntIndex and* numOfBeams (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_15346\_replaced([11411607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-avvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

The average long-term CFO (IE *longTermCfoMetric)* is not used.\*\*

IE *foeValid in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq indicates if long-term FOE is vaid and shall be used for CFO. If *foeValid=false, frequency offset correction shall be skipped.*\*\*

The CFO estimation and compensation algorithms on PUSCH are described in section 2.3.3 of "5GMax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

As PTRS is not supported in L1 in eCPRI 7.2e, only DMRS-based FOE method is supported. FOE algorithm is performed under the following condition:

If  (numOfDmrsSymbols ≥ 2)

If (highSpeedCell == TRUE)

Process FOE on the 2 last DMRS symbols and skip the first DMRS

Else

Process FOE on the first 2 DMRS symbols, and skip the remaining DMRS

Endif

Else

skip FOE

set ST FOE metric to  “0”

Endif

where

* parameter *numOfDmrsSymbols is the number of DMRS symbols per slot and is obtained by procedure described in 5G\_L1\_13606\_replaced([11412127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e95aofvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

**- flag high\_speed\_cell is given at component carrier set-up in class *CombiningLinkConf  (see L1L\_SW\_4811).***

The requirement is valid for up to 8 paired UEs per PRB.

---

###### 7.4.5.12.1.1.2 Odin

**7.4.5.12.1.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12649473`)

Odin
Carrier Frequency Offset (CFO) estimation and compensation shall be performed on PUSCH on Odin-RU.

Upon reception of the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message provided by L2-PS via L1-BB, L1-RU shall get beam-wise long-term CFO estimate using the metric* longTermCfoMetricOfBeam *contained in this message. The estimate shall be then used to compensate the CFO on the received PUSCH signal on the appropriate spatial streams (expected at the SFN and NR-slot specified in the same* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message).\*\*\*\*

The relationship between the elements of  *longTermCfoMetricOfBeam, beams* and spatial streams is given in the table below.\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | LT FOE for antenna j | Beam ID | (e)CPRI spatial streams | First supporting feature |
| C16’2, [CB012115-SR-HA1] C16'4, C16'8 [End CB012115-SR-HA1] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | patternId[0] | streams *startAntIndex &* startAndIndex+1\*\* | CB012115-SR-HA |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | patternId[1] | streams *startAntIndex+2 &* startAndIndex+3\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | patternId[2] | streams *startAntIndex+4 &* startAndIndex+5\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | patternId[3] | streams *startAntIndex+6 &* startAndIndex+7\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[4] | patternId[4] | streams *startAntIndex+8 &* startAndIndex+9\*\* | CB012115-SR-HA |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[5] | patternId[5] | streams *startAntIndex+10 &* startAndIndex+11\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[6] | patternId[6] | streams *startAntIndex+12 &* startAndIndex+13\*\* |  |  |
| longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[7] | patternId[7] | streams *startAntIndex+14 &* startAndIndex+15\*\* |  |  |

L2-PS provides beam-wise LT-CFO metrics only for the allocated beams of the UE. CFO estimation shall be performed only on the owned streams of the UE, determined by parameters *startAntIndex and* numOfBeams (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_15346\_replaced([11411607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-avvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

The average long-term CFO (IE *longTermCfoMetric)* is not used.\*\*

IE *foeValid in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq indicates if long-term FOE is vaid and shall be used for CFO. If *foeValid=false, frequency offset correction shall be skipped.*\*\*

The CFO estimation and compensation algorithms on PUSCH are described in section 2.3.3 of "5GMax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

As PTRS is not supported in L1 in eCPRI 7.2e, only DMRS-based FOE method is supported. FOE algorithm is performed under the following condition:

If  (numOfDmrsSymbols ≥ 2)

Process FOE on the first 2 DMRS symbols, and skip the remaining DMRSs

Else

skip FOE

set ST FOE metric to  “0”

Endif

where parameter *numOfDmrsSymbols is the number of DMRS symbols per slot and is obtained by procedure described in 5G\_L1\_13606\_replaced([11412127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e95aofvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

[CB012115-SR-HA1] The requirement is valid for up to 4 paired UEs per PRB. [End CB012115-SR-HA1]

##### 7.4.5.12.1.2 FOE protection

###### 7.4.5.12.1.2.0-2 FOE protection If one of the beam-wise long-term CFO longTermCfoMetricOfBeam received from L2-PS has complex value 0 (0+j0), L1-RU shall consider that long-term CFO is 0 Hz for the corresponding spatial streams. L1-RU shall then proceed with CFO estimation assuming longTermCfoMetricOfBeam=1+j0.** [CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA] (ID: 12649554)

##### 7.4.5.12.1.3 DMRS-base FOE

###### 7.4.5.12.1.3.1 Thor

**7.4.5.12.1.3.1.0-3**  (ID: `12525919`)

Thor
12525919:

12525919:

12525919:
Thor
In DMRS based FOE, rotation between DMRS symbols is detected

In CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM non-HST case this is measured by using 2 first DMRS. If there are 3 DMRS symbols, still only 2 first ones are used.

In high-speed cell case, 3 DMRS symbols are always configured. Rotation is measured between the two last DMRS symbols (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_901\_replaced([11102573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knj4DPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Calculation is defined in sections 2.3.3.2 for CP-OFDM and 2.3.3.8.2 for DFT-S-OFDM of "5gmax algorithm specification", and calculation is same.

Calculation is done in multiple steps and below is part of step 3, which shows that difference between two DMRS symbols is detected:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation defines $C\_{ST}^{raw}$ as a sum over three indices. The first index, `ant`, ranges from 0 to $N\_{RX}-1$. The second index, `l`, ranges from 0 to $N\_{layer}^{NDMRS}-1$. The third index, `r`, belongs to the set $SCSet\_l^{DMRS}$. The equation also includes a fraction where the numerator is $H\_{S\_l^{DMRS}(2),l,r,ant}^{raw}$ multiplied by the conjugate of $H\_{S\_l^{DMRS}(1),l,r,ant}^{raw}$, and the denominator is $\sigma\_{noise,ant}^2$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Note that noise is taken also into account in above formula.

Antenna specific calculation is done when *N*RX=4. In that case, antenna specific values [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a stylized font. The expression is "C" followed by a fraction. The numerator of the fraction is "ant" and the denominator is "st". The entire expression is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and summed value [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains text that appears to be "C'au ST". The text is in a stylized font, with the "C" being large and curved, and the "au" appearing above the "ST". The letters are white against a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] are calculated:\*\*

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$C\_{ST}^{ant} = \sum\_{l=0}^{N\_{layer}^{DMRS}-1} \sum\_{r \in ScSet\_{l}^{DMRS}} \frac{H\_{S\_{l}^{DMRS}(2),l,r,ant}^{raw} \left( H\_{S\_{l}^{DMRS}(1),l,r,ant}^{raw} \right)^\*}{\sigma\_{noise,ant}^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

[image-4][image\_desc]$C\_{ST}^{raw} = \sum\_{ant=0}^{N\_{rx}-1} C\_{ST}^{ant}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains text that appears to be "C'au ST". The text is in a stylized font, with the "C" being large and curved, and the "au" appearing above the "ST". The letters are white against a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] is raw FOE. Final FOE value [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "CST" in a stylized font. The letters are white and appear to be outlined in black. The background is a solid black rectangle.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]shall contain [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains text that appears to be "C'au ST". The text is in a stylized font, with the "C" being large and curved, and the "au" appearing above the "ST". The letters are white against a black background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7] and long-term FOE [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Crr" in a stylized font. The letters are in a dark color, possibly black or dark gray, against a white background. The letters are slightly blurred, giving them a soft appearance. The text is enclosed within a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] (if *foeValid is set to 'true' in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message), as indicated in "5GMax algorithm specification" § 2.3.3.2:\*\*

[image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$C\_{ST} = |C\_{ST}^{aw}| \cdot \exp \left( j \cdot \left( \text{angle}(C\_{ST}^{aw}) \cdot \frac{Itv}{S\_{l}^{DMRS}(2) - S\_{l}^{DMRS}(1)} + \text{angle}(C\_{LT}) \right) \right)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2342.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]

where *Itv is the symbol interval between two symbols in the short-term correlation computation. This is a hard-coded parameter set to 4.*

[CB014106-SR-A] 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall further perform maximum FOE protection on total FO to avoid overflow, using foeGapLargest  IE of PuschReceiveReqGrant, as specified in section [#sec-PuschFreqOffEstUpdVer](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-PuschFreqOffEstUpdVer) of 5GMax Algorithm Specification.

The maximum value Cap is defined as

[image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a stylized font. The equation is:
$Cap = \frac{Itv}{foeGapLargest} \times \pi \times Scalar$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/foeGapLargest.png[/image\_path][/image-10]

where Scalar is the adjustment factor and shall be set to 0.99 according to 5GMax recommendation. FOE protection shall be performed as follows:

[image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$C\_{ST} = |C\_{ST}^{raw}| \exp(j(\min(\text{angle}(C\_{ST}^{raw})\frac{Itv}{FoeGap} + \text{angle}(C\_{LT}), Cap)))$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04161555.png[/image\_path][/image-11],

and

[image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$C\_{ST}^{ant,report} = |C\_{ST}^{ant}| \exp(j(\min(\text{angle}(C\_{ST}^{ant}) \frac{Itv}{FoeGap} + \text{angle}(C\_{LT}^{ant}, Cap))))$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04161555.png[/image\_path][/image-12],

where,

[image-13][image\_desc]FoeGap = $S\_{l}^{DMRS}(2) - S\_{l}^{DMRS}(1)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04161554.png[/image\_path][/image-13].

[End CB014106-SR-A]

Antenna-wise short-term FOE is sent to L2-PS via L1-BB in IE *shoftTermCfoMetricOfAnt of mesage* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.\*\*

Combined short-term FOE is sent in IE *shortTermCfoMetric of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.\*\*

#### 7.4.5.12.2 Phase Noise Estimation

##### 7.4.5.12.2.1 PNE selection

###### 7.4.5.12.2.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.12.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11413144`)

Thor
On Thor-RU, only DMRS-based phase noise estimation (PNE) is supported.

DMRS-based PNE is performed if the following conditions are met:

* Long-term CFO is not valid - i.e. forValid=false in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.
* 2 or more DMRS symbols are configured - numOfDmrsSymbols>=2 where numOfDmrsSymbols is determined as described in 5G\_L1\_13606\_replaced([11412127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e95aofvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Otherwise, PNE is skipped.

---

###### 7.4.5.12.2.1.2 Odin

**7.4.5.12.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12649561`)

Odin
On Odin-RU, only DMRS-based phase noise estimation (PNE) is supported.

DMRS-based PNE is performed if the following conditions are met:

* Long-term CFO is not valid - i.e. *forValid=false in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.\*\*

*- 2 or more DMRS symbols are configured -* numOfDmrsSymbols>=2 where *numOfDmrsSymbols is determined as described in 5G\_L1\_13606\_replaced([11412127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e95aofvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*

Otherwise, PNE is skipped.

---

**7.4.5.12.2.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11413167`)

DMRS based PNE is described in chapter 2.3.9.1 and 2.3.9.5.1 of "5GMax algorithm specification" for CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM respectively. Algorithm is actually the same in both case.

Input for DMRS based PNE is short-term DMRS-based FOE (CST) which is calculated in 5G\_L1\_13607\_replaced([11413031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9-TIvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is first changed to frequency offset, as described by formula 2-73:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$\delta f = \frac{angle(C\_{ST})}{2\pi \cdot ltv \cdot (N\_{FFT} + N\_{CP}) \cdot T\_s}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2347.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a black and white rendering of the mathematical expression "81". The "8" is on the left and the "1" is on the right, slightly higher than the "8".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2347.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is then used to calculate PN for every symbol and antenna (if antenna based FOEs are present) as presented in the formula below (2-225):

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
$PN\_{i,l,ant} = 2\pi (N\_{0,i}^{gap} - N\_{0,s\_i^{DMRS}(1)}^{gap}) \cdot T\_s \cdot \delta\hat{f} = 2\pi \cdot N\_{s\_i^{DMRS}(1)}^{gap} \cdot T\_s \cdot \delta\hat{f}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2347.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

Based on this formula, PN increases for every symbol.

### 7.4.5.13 FOC &amp; PNC

#### 7.4.5.13.1 Frequency Offset Compensation

##### 7.4.5.13.1.0-1 Frequency Offset Compensation In the next update, split 5G_L1_13611_replaced( 11413189 ) into Inter- and Intra-symbol FOC, keep Inter-symbol FOC under this title, and create Intra-symbol FOC requirement under 5G_L1_13610_replaced( 11412640 ) (Frond-end Processing). (ID: 11413183)

##### 7.4.5.13.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.13.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12703877`)

Thor
(Since 25R3) FOC (Frequency Offset Correction)

[Before PR831459-25R3]FOC (Frequency Offset Correction) is done by using long-term CFO (LT-CFO) which is received in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message when foeValid==True. If LT-CFO is present, there are two different kinds of FOCs: intra-symbol FOC and inter-symbol FOC.

[PR831459-25R3]  
If LT-CFO is present, there are two different kinds of FOCs: intra-symbol FOC and inter-symbol FOC.

Inter-symbol FOC (Frequency Offset Correction) is done by using long-term CFO (LT-CFO)  longTermCfoMetricOfBeam by L1-RU which is received in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message when foeValid==True.

Intra-symbol FOC (Frequency Offset Correction) is done by using long-term CFO (LT-CFO) longTermCfoMetric by L1-BB which is received in UlData\_PuschReceiverReq message when foeValid==True.  
[End PR831459-25R3]

FOC algorithm is defined in section 2.3.3.6 of "5gmax algorithm specification". Algorithm is same for CP-OFDM and DFT-S-OFDM.

Intra-Symbol FOC makes correction per symbol, and each subcarrier has different correction. This is realised by using 5 or 11 tap filter. Only 11-tap filter is supported on Thor-RU.

Inter-Symbol FOC is adjustment per symbol, and each subcarrier has same correction, but symbols have different value.

Correction is done per antenna.

In L1-RU, intra-symbol FOC is performed on DMRS symbols before raw channel estimation. Inter-symbol FOC is done in ARXE MHAB.

Intra-symbol FOC on data symbol is done in L1-BB.

---

##### 7.4.5.13.1.2 Odin

**7.4.5.13.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12654589`)

Odin
FOC (Frequency Offset Correction)

FOC (Frequency Offset Correction) is done by using long-term CFO (LT-CFO) which is received in *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message longTermCfoMetric in UlData\_PuschReceiverReq message when* foeValid==True.\*\*

If LT-CFO is present, there are two different kinds of FOCs: intra-symbol FOC and inter-symbol FOC.

FOC algorithm is defined in section 2.3.3.6 of "5gmax algorithm specification". Algorithm is same for CP-OFDM and DFT-S-OFDM.

Intra-Symbol FOC makes correction per symbol, and each subcarrier has different correction. This is realised by using 5 or 11 tap filter. Only 11-tap filter is supported on Thor-RU [CB012115-SR-HA] and Odin-RU [End CB012115-SR-HA].

Inter-Symbol FOC is adjustment per symbol, and each subcarrier has same correction, but symbols have different value.

Correction is done per antenna.

In L1-RU, intra-symbol FOC is performed on DMRS symbols before raw channel estimation. Inter-symbol FOC is done in ARXE MHAB.

Intra-symbol FOC on data symbol is done in L1-BB.

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

---

#### 7.4.5.13.2 FOC Optimization

**7.4.5.13.2.0-1**  (ID: `12524113`)

FOC Optimization
5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall perform Intra-symbol FOC optimization for FDD FR1 as follows.

1. If High-Speed Train (HST) mode if inactive, that is, when high\_speed\_cell IE of CombiningLinkConf ([11630917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_sTQh5tnCEe26EtvmdlGL5w)) is False, the FOC optimization method for DMRS symbols shall be set to "Real".

2. If High-Speed Train (HST) mode if active, that is, when high\_speed\_cell IE of CombiningLinkConf ([11630917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_sTQh5tnCEe26EtvmdlGL5w)) is True, the FOC optimization method for DMRS symbols shall be set to "On".

The details of optimization methods are described in section [#sec-PuschFreqOffComUpdVer](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-PuschFreqOffComUpdVer) of "5GMax – 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification."

Note: Intra-symbol FOC for data symbols is performed on DU side in DMAP.

---

#### 7.4.5.13.3 Phase Noise Compensation

**7.4.5.13.3.0-2**  (ID: `12654597`)

Phase Noise Compensation
On Thor RU [CB012115-SR-HA] and Odin RU [End CB012115-SR-HA] , only DMRS-based PNC is supported.

DMRS-based PNC is performed in ARXE MHAB when DMRS-based PNE is calculated, under the conditions specified in 5G\_L1\_13617\_replaced([11413137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9-TJvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Input is PNE described in 5G\_L1\_13619\_replaced([11413150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9-TKPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PNC algorithm is defined in chapter 2.3.9.2 of "5GMax algorithm specification" for CP-OFDM and is chapter 2.3.9.5.1.2 and 2.3.9.5.2.2 for DFT-S-OFDM.

Algoritm is same for CP-OFDM and DFT-S-OFDM when PNE is calculated from DMRS.

---

#### 7.4.5.14 SU/MU IRC receiver

##### 7.4.5.14.1 Overview

###### 7.4.5.14.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.14.1.1.0-5**  (ID: `11413243`)

Thor
**PUSCH IRC SU and MU receiver algorithm for FR1 in eCPRI 7.2e**

For Thor-RU L1 HW, MMSE-IRC receiver is used when following subcell types are configured during L1 cell setup:

**[Before CB008235-SR-X]- C4'2 (TDD 4RX IRC)**[End CB008235-SR-X]\*\*\*\*

For Thor-RU L1 HW, MMSE-IRC receiver is used. IRC size depends on subcell type and MIMO configuration:

**[Before CB008235-SR-X]- If subcell type is C4'2, 4RX IRC is used.**[End CB008235-SR-X]\*\*\*\*

* If subcell type is C16’2 or C16’4 and UE is configured in SU-MIMO, then IRC order (8RX or 16 RX) is selected by

ueReceiverSize from PuschReceiveReqGrant structure in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB008235-A]**

* If subcell type is C16'8 and UE is configured in SU-MIMO, 8RX IRC is used.

**[End CB008235-A]**

* If subcell type is C16'4 or **[CB008235-A] C16'8** [End CB008235-A] and UEs are paired in MU-MIMO, 16RX IRC is used.\*\*\*\*

MMSE-IRC shrinkage receiver is used with 4Rx.

Shrinkage and hybrid IRC are supported for 8Rx and 16Rx.

When there are multiple DMRS symbols, all DMRS symbols are used and averaged for the calculation of the disturbance matrix *R*dd.\*\*

Refer to “5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification” section "2.3.6.2 MMSE-IRC algorithm specification" for more details.

---

###### 7.4.5.14.1.2 Odin

**7.4.5.14.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12654645`)

Odin
**PUSCH IRC SU [CB012115-HA1] and MU [End CB012115-HA1] receiver algorithm for FR1 in eCPRI 7.2e**

For Odin-RU L1 HW, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall implement MMSE-IRC receiver. IRC size depends on the subcell type and MIMO configuration:

* If subcell type is C16'2 and UE is configured in SU-MIMO, [Before CB012115-HA1] 8RX IRC is used [CB12115-HA1] then IRC order (8RX or 16 RX) is selected by *ueReceiverSize from PuschReceiveReqGrant structure in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message ([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*
* If subcell type is C16'2 or C16'4 and UEs are paired in MU-MIMO, 16RX IRC is used. [End CB012115-HA1]

Shrinkage and hybrid IRC shall be supported for 8Rx [CB012115-HA1] and 16Rx. [End CB012115-HA1]

When there are multiple DMRS symbols, all DMRS symbols are used and averaged for the calculation of the disturbance matrix *R*dd.\*\*

Refer to “5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification” section "2.3.6.2 MMSE-IRC algorithm specification" for more details.

---

##### 7.4.5.14.2 Rdd matrix estimation

###### 7.4.5.14.2.1 Thor

**7.4.5.14.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413260`)

Thor
The computation of covariance matrix (Rdd) is given by Rdd = E{d\*d^H}, where vector d is the channel-based disturbance. Refer to “5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification” section "2.3.6.2 MMSE-IRC algorithm specification" for more details.

[CB008235-A] The requirement is also valid for PUSCH 8 layers case [CB008235-B] with TD-PDP or mixture PDP algorithm for PDP length determination as described in 5G\_L1\_18576\_replaced([11412929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99sEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008235-B] [End CB008235-A]

Note: Using Raw CEs is expected to be mathematically equivalent to using the received signal and it simplifies algorithm implementation.

---

###### 7.4.5.14.2.2 Odin

###### 7.4.5.14.2.2.0-1 Odin The computation of covariance matrix (Rdd) is given by Rdd = E{d*d^H}, where vector d is the received signal data based disturbance. Note: Using Raw CEs is expected to be mathematically equivalent to using the received signal and it simplifies algorithm implementation. (ID: 12813868)

##### 7.4.5.14.3 Rdd matrix processing

###### 7.4.5.14.3.1 Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd debiasing

**7.4.5.14.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `12815511`)

Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd debiasing
When *rdd\_debiasing in* CombiningLinkConf*(L1L\_SW\_4811) is true, and only Shrinkage algorithm is used and Legalization is effectively deactivated, that is,*\*\*

* if *rdHybridIrcEnabledFlag = 0, when*ueReceiverSize = 8, or\*\*
* if *rdHybridIrcEnabledFlag16Rx = 0, when*ueReceiverSize = 16,\*\*

then 5G-L1-UL(Radio) shall apply the debiasing of covariance matirx (Rdd) with a scaling factor which helps to mitigate the underestimation of Rdd matrix elements.

Refer to [#eq-PuschMmseIrcRddDebias](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#eq-PuschMmseIrcRddDebias) in 5GMAX Algorithm Specification for more details.

5G-L1-UL(Radio) shall ignore rdd\_debiasing when Hybrid Rdd estimation (Shrinkage+Legalization) is performed and shall not perform Rdd Debiasing.

The requirement is supported in Thor. [CB012115-HA] It shall also be supported in Odin. [End CB012115-HA]

---

###### 7.4.5.14.3.2 Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd averaging

**7.4.5.14.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11413289`)

Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd averaging
When rdd\_averaging\_prb\_size in CombiningLinkConf  (L1L\_SW\_4811) is larger than 0 and ueReceiverSize in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_15101\_replaced([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 16, 5G-L1-UL(Radio) shall average the computed covariance matrix (Rdd) over rdd\_averaging\_prb\_size PRBs which helps to stablize the Rdd matrix before inversion.

Note:

1. In case of MU MIMO, Rdd averaging is conducted per virtual UE.
2. large rdd\_averaging\_prb\_size may affect the performance of narrowband interference mitigation via Rdd group scaling algorithm (See 5G\_L1\_18655\_replaced([11413294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9_hQvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Refer to 5GMAX algorithm specification document chapter 2.3.6.2 for more details.

---

###### 7.4.5.14.3.3 Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd group scaling

**7.4.5.14.3.3.0-4**  (ID: `12813870`)

Convariance matrix (Rdd) optimization: Rdd group scaling
When *subcell\_Type (L1L\_SW\_4811) is not C4\_2 and* ueReceiverSize in **UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq ([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is 8 or 16, 5G-L1-UL(Radio) shall perform covariance matrix (Rdd) Group Scaling in Thor using the advanced method called ['OPT5+'](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ATFL1Spec/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7B5DE62EE4-BF06-44EA-8285-5B46B78E5156%7D&file=Improvement%20for%20ARXL%20handle%20narrowband%20interference%201.pptx&action=edit&mobileredirect=true). This can avoid to loose precision in case of narrowband interference scenario.**\*\*

[CB012115-HA] In Odin, the group scaling is only needed for optional eFXP. The default format is IQFP, for which group scaling is not required. [End CB012115-HA]

Refer to 5GMAX algorithm specification document chapter [#sec-PuschMmseIrc](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-PuschMmseIrc) for more details.

---

##### 7.4.5.14.4 Equalization

###### 7.4.5.14.4.1 Supported Equalization Types

###### 7.4.5.14.4.1.1 Thor

**7.4.5.14.4.1.1.0-3**  (ID: `11413341`)

Thor
Supported equalization types

The supported equalization types on PUSCH are:

* 2 layers MIMO equalization for 2 layers spatial multiplexing,
* 4 layers MIMO equalization for up to 4 UEs per PRB for C16'4 subcell
* [CB008235-A] 8 layers MIMO equalization for up to 8 UEs per PRB for C16'8 subcell [End CB008235-A]
* SIMO equalization for 1 layer spatial multiplexing
* SIMO equalization for singleTx.

The normalization factor in equalization is averaged per symbol.

The information needed to choose the equalization type are the number of layers (numOfLayers) and the spacial configuration (spatialMode) parameters that come within the UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The equalization algorithm is described in section 2.3.6 of '5GMax algorithm specification'.

---

###### 7.4.5.14.4.1.2 Odin

**7.4.5.14.4.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12655684`)

Odin
**Supported equalization types**

The supported equalization types on PUSCH are:

* 2 layers MIMO equalization for 2 layers spatial multiplexing,
* [CB012115-HA1] 4 layers MIMO equalization for up to 4 UEs per PRB **for C16'4 subcell**[End CB012115-HA1]\*\*\*\*
* SIMO equalization for 1 layer spatial multiplexing
* SIMO equalization for singleTx.

The normalization factor in equalization is averaged per symbol.

The information needed to choose the equalization type are the number of layers (*numOfLayers)* and the spacial configuration (*spatialMode)* parameters that come within the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message described in [11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*\*\*\*\*

---

###### 7.4.5.14.4.3 Single Antenna Transmission for RAR UL

###### 7.4.5.14.4.3.0-2 Single Antenna Transmission for RAR UL Specific case for PUSCH scheduled by RAR (Random Access Request) UL grant during random access On Thor-RU [CB012115-SR-HA] and Odin-RU [End CB012115-SR-HA], the single antenna transmission in UL shall be also supported to decode PUSCH scheduled by RAR UL grant during the random access procedure. For this scheme, SIMO equalization is described in section 2.3.5.1 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G_L1_2794) shall be applied. (ID: 12656058)

### 7.4.5.15 ML-based channel estimation

#### 7.4.5.15.1 Pro-processing

#### 7.4.5.15.2 ML model

#### 7.4.5.15.3 Post-processing

### 7.4.5.16 DeepRx receiver

## 7.4.6 Measurements

### 7.4.6.1 Overview

#### 7.4.6.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413435`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL shall use raw channel estimates based on only the first DMRS port in each CDM group (refer to 5G\_L1\_13590\_replaced([11412892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FCfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to compute the measurements including time offset (5G\_L1\_15374\_replaced([11413448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-AIXvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), carrier frequency offset (5G\_L1\_15393\_replaced([11413491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-AvZ_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), received interference and themal noise power (5G\_L1\_13450\_replaced([11493863](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDVvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RSSI (5G\_L1\_13457\_replaced([11413852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CklPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), received signal power (5G\_L1\_13919\_replaced([11493870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDV_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SINR (5G\_L1\_14002\_replaced([11413792](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9ivvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and post equalized SU SINR (5G\_L1\_16485\_replaced([11413767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9hvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB008235-A] The requirement is also valid for PUSCH 8 layers case. [End CB008235-A]

[CB008235-B] When mixture PDP algorithm is activated (5G\_L1\_18576\_replaced([11412929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99sEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the spatial stream wise measurements are computed from time domain for UE's own beam(s) and from the frequency domain for other beam(s). [End CB008235-B]

[CB010708-G-UPD002] When split-panel beamforming is activated (5G\_L1\_16910\_replaced([11412389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e96oxvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a scaling factor scomp according to suSplitpanelMode in UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_15101\_replaced([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be applied to compensate the measurements including received interference and themal noise power, RSSI, and received signal power. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor scomp . [End CB010708-G-UPD002]

Note:

1. Using Raw CEs is expected to be mathematically equivalent to using the received signal and it simplifies algorithm implementation.

[CB010708-G-UPD002] 2. The measurement compensation only impacts noisePower, noisePerPrb, rxPower, rxPowerOfAnt rssi, linRssiOfAnt, and linNoiseOfAnt. It doesn't apply to shortTermCfoMetrixReal, shortTermCfoMetrixImag, shortTermTaMetric, shortTermTaPeakAmp, sinr, shortTermCfoMetrixRealOfAnt, shortTermCfoMetrixImagOfAnt, shortTermTaMetricOfAnt, shortTermTaPeakAmpsinrOfAnt, and sinrOfAnt. [End CB010708-G-UPD002]

---

#### 7.4.6.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12813877`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL shall use raw channel estimates based on only the first DMRS port in each CDM group (refer to [11412892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FCfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to compute the measurements including time offset ([11413448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-AIXvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), carrier frequency offset ([11413491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-AvZ_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), received interference and thermal noise power ([11493863](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDVvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), RSSI ([11413852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CklPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), received signal power ([11493870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDV_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), SINR ([11413792](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9ivvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and post equalized SU SINR ([11413767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9hvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When split-panel beamforming is activated ([11412389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e96oxvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), a scaling factor *s*comp according to *suSplitpanelMode in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq ([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*shall be applied to compensate the measurements including received interference and thermal noise power, RSSI, and received signal power. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor* s*comp .***\***\*

Note:

1. Using Raw CEs is expected to be mathematically equivalent to using the received signal and it simplifies algorithm implementation.
2. The measurement compensation only impacts *noisePower, noisePerPrb, rxPower, rxPowerOfAnt rssi, linRssiOfAnt, and* linNoiseOfAnt. It doesn't apply to *shortTermCfoMetrixReal, shortTermCfoMetrixImag, shortTermTaMetric, shortTermTaPeakAmp, sinr, shortTermCfoMetrixRealOfAnt, shortTermCfoMetrixImagOfAnt, shortTermTaMetricOfAnt, shortTermTaPeakAmpsinrOfAnt, and* sinrOfAnt.\*\*\*\*

### 7.4.6.2 Time Alignment

#### 7.4.6.2.1 Timing offset report

##### 7.4.6.2.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.2.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413460`)

Thor
L1-RU estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on PUSCH as described in 5G\_L1\_13599\_replaced([11412856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FAvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Timing offset is reported to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and is used for updating the timing advance (TA) measurement.

A combined value shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS for both TA IE shortTermTaMetric (TO position) and shortTermTaPeakAmp (TO peak amplitude). The reported shortTermTaMetric value is in unit of (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Antenna-wise TO information elements are also reported in structures fhPuschAntMeas of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs in fields shoftTermTaMetricOfAnt and shoftTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt. Unit of shortTermTaMetricOfAnt is also of  (1/2μ) \* Ts (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15103\_replaced([11517124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8N_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB010708-C, CB010708-E] In case of MU receiver, antenna-wise and combined TO information shall be computed only on UE own spatial streams (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB010708-C, CB010708-E]

The algorithm for combining TO metric and peak amplitude is described in section 2.7.6 of "5GMax algorithm specification".

---

##### 7.4.6.2.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12656079`)

Odin
L1-RU estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on PUSCH as described in [11412856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FAvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). Timing offset is reported to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and is used for updating the timing advance (TA) measurement.*

A combined value shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS for both TA IE *shortTermTaMetric (TO position) and* shortTermTaPeakAmp (TO peak amplitude). The reported *shortTermTaMetric value is in unit of (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*\*\*

Antenna-wise TO information elements are also reported in structures *fhPuschAntMeas of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs in fields *shoftTermTaMetricOfAnt and* shoftTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt. Unit of *shortTermTaMetricOfAnt is also of  (1/2μ) \* Ts (see [11517124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8N_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, antenna-wise and combined TO information shall be computed only on UE own spatial streams (see [11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CB012115-HA1]\*\*\*\*

The algorithm for combining TO metric and peak amplitude is described in section 2.7.6 of "5GMax algorithm specification".

---

#### 7.4.6.2.2 Invalid value

**7.4.6.2.2.0-3**  (ID: `12656093`)

Invalid value
For PUSCH, L1-RU shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise TOE (*shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) and its associated peak amplitude (*shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt) in message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs* in at least one of the following conditions:\*\*\*\*

* timing offset fo the corresponding spatial stream is not in the allowed range (see 5G\_L1\_13997\_replaced([11412851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FAfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* the corresponding spatial stream is not in the set of allocated streams for the UE (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

L1-RU shall report invalid measurement for combined TOE (*shortTermTaMetric) and its associated peak amplitude (*shortTermTaPeakAmp) in at least one of the following conditions:\*\*

* the combined TOE metric is out of the allowed range (see 5G\_L1\_13997\_replaced([11412851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99FAfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

Invalid value of *shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and* shortTermTaMetric shall be set to −32768. Invalid value of *shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt and* shortTermTaMetric shall be set to −1.\*\*\*\*

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

---

### 7.4.6.3 Carrier Frequency Offset

#### 7.4.6.3.1 Frequency offset estimation report

##### 7.4.6.3.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.3.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413503`)

Thor
For Thor-RU and SU [CB010708-C] or MU [End CB010708-C] receiver

For each scheduled UE, L1-RU shall estimate an antenna-wise ST FOE (see 5G\_L1\_13607\_replaced([11413031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9-TIvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and report it to L2-PS via L1-BB in  IEs shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt in antena-wise structures puschAntMeas of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_202\_replaced([11513842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB010708-C, CB010708-E] In case of MU receiver, ST-FOE is estimated only on the spatial streams allocated to the UE (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB010708-C, CB010708-E]

The mapping of structures puschAntMeas to spatial streams and beams is defined in 5G\_L1\_14004\_replaced([11413817](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9jvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

L1-RU also estimates average ST-FOE across spatial streams [CB010708-C, CB010708-E] allocated to the UE [End CB010708-C, CB010708-E] which is sent to L1-BB and L2-PS in IE shortTermCfoMetric in message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.

---

##### 7.4.6.3.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.3.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12656096`)

Odin
For Odin-RU and SU receiver

For each scheduled UE, L1-RU shall estimate an antenna-wise ST FOE (see 5G\_L1\_13607\_replaced([11413031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9-TIvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and report it to L2-PS via L1-BB in  IEs *shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt in antena-wise structures* puschAntMeas of message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_202\_replaced([11513842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*.\*\*\*\*

[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, ST-FOE is estimated only on the spatial streams allocated to the UE (see [11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB012115-HA1]

The mapping of structures *puschAntMeas to spatial streams and beams is defined in [12657377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_sTuNkEihEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ).*

L1-RU also estimates average ST-FOE across spatial streams which is sent to L1-BB and L2-PS in IE *shortTermCfoMetric in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.\*\*

---

#### 7.4.6.3.2 Invalid value

**7.4.6.3.2.0-3**  (ID: `12815310`)

Invalid value
L1-RU shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise FOE (*shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt) in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs *when the corresponding spatial stream is not in the set of own UE spatial streams for MU receiver.*\*\*

Invalid value of *shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt shall be set to 0+0j (both real and imaginary parts set to zero).*

The requirement is supported in Thor. [CB012115-HA1] It shall also be supported in Odin. [End CB012115-HA1]

---

### 7.4.6.4 Received Signal Power

#### 7.4.6.4.1 Combined Received Signal Power

**7.4.6.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12656098`)

Combined Received Signal Power
**Combined received signal power**

L1-RU shall estimate a combined UL received power on DMRS over all receiving spatial streams for each scheduled UE. It shall report it to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB within the IE *rxPower of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs for long term (LT) averaging. The *rxPower element is delivered in dBm unit as illustrated in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*

~~When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio for all the receiving spatial streams (eg. broken antenna scenario), L1-RU shall set the~~ ~~rxPower~~ ~~parameter in~~ ~~UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs~~ ~~message to INVALID value (-140dBm).~~

The RX power estimation algorithm for PUSCH is described in section 2.7.4.1 of "5Gmax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

---

Receiver signal Power computation (measurement M4)
**Signal power computation (measurement M4)**

For a given user *u, antenna-wise RX power in linear scale is derived from antenna-wise RSSI [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is "M 1\_norm,a(u)". The text is in a dark color against a white background. The font is a sans-serif font. The expression appears to be a single line of text.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2410.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] (see 5G\_L1\_13974\_replaced([11413887](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CkmfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and antenna-wise noise noise [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in black text on a white background. The expression is: $K \mathbf{1}\_{norm,a}(u)$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2410.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] (see 5G\_L1\_13972\_replaced([11413664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-BWe_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):*

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M\_{4\_a}(u) = \frac{M1\_{norm,a}(u) - K1\_{norm,a}(u)}{S^2\_{DMRSBoost,PUSCH}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2410.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

where [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a subscript format. The main symbol is 'S' with a superscript '2'. The subscript is a combination of letters and words: 'DMRSBoost,PUSCH'.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2410.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the power boose factor for PUSCH DMRS (see 5G\_L1\_13974\_replaced([11413887](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CkmfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Combined RX power is then obtained by summing antenna-wise contributions:

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M\_4(u) = \frac{\sum\_{a=0}^{N\_{Rx}-1} M\_1\_{norm,a}(u) - K\_1\_{norm,a}(u)}{S\_{DMRSBoost,PUSCH}^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2410.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

Note: as signal power is computed from receiver interference and themal noise power (5G\_L1\_13450\_replaced([11493863](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDVvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PUSCH RSSI (5G\_L1\_13457\_replaced([11413852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CklPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the compensation in case of split-panel beamforming is conducted automatically. No extra operation is requested.

Before being reported to upper layer, antenna-wise RX power and combined RX power should be converted to dBm unit and PUSCH scaling factor shall be applied, as described in 5G\_L1\_8903\_replaced([11421828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFvfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

#### 7.4.6.4.3 Receiver signal Power computation (measurement M4_ant)

**7.4.6.4.3.0-3**  (ID: `12656127`)

Receiver signal Power computation (measurement M4\_ant)
**Antenna-wise received signal power**

L1-RU shall estimate antenna-wise UL received power on DMRS associated to PUSCH for each UE and report it to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB within the IE *rxPowerOfAnt sent in structure* fhPuschAntMeas of message *UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs. The* rxPowerOfAnt parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15103\_replaced([11517124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8N_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

Note: as signal power is computed from receiver interference and themal noise power (5G\_L1\_13450\_replaced([11493863](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEkDVvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PUSCH RSSI (5G\_L1\_13457\_replaced([11413852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CklPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the compensation in case of split-panel beamforming is conducted automatically. No extra operation is requested.

PUSCH antenna-wise rx power is estimated as described in section 2.7.4.1 of "5Gmax algorithm specification" **(see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

---

### 7.4.6.5 Received Interference and Noise Power

#### 7.4.6.5.1 Noise power report

##### 7.4.6.5.1.0-1 Noise power report Duplicate Requirement (Notice! Unit has changed to dbm.) L1 Radio shall compute and report noise power estimation per PRB on all scheduled PRBs. The unit of these noise measurements is aW (1e-18 W). (ID: 11413628)

##### 7.4.6.5.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.5.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413641`)

Thor
For each configured subcell, L1-RU shall estimate the noise (interference + thermal noise) power for all the allocated PRBs.

Reported noise power per sub-cell (on allocated PUSCH PRBs) is the noise power normalized to 1 PRB, combined over all receiving spatial streams.

[CB010708-C, CB010708-E] In case of MU receiver, only the spatial streams allocated to each UE shall be considered for unused REs (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For used REs, all spatial streams are always used. [End CB010708-C, CB010708-E]

Noise power per subcell is reported to L2-PS via L1-BB in field noisePower of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespCellPs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14996\_replaced([11517087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVMPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Unit is dBm and granularity of the reported value is 0.1 dBm.

Noise power computation is described in section 2.7.3.1 of "5GMax algorithm specification".

---

##### 7.4.6.5.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.5.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12656135`)

Odin
For each configured subcell, L1-RU shall estimate the noise (interference + thermal noise) power for all the allocated PRBs.

Reported noise power per sub-cell (on allocated PUSCH PRBs) is the noise power normalized to 1 PRB, combined over all receiving spatial streams.

[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, only the spatial streams allocated to each UE shall be considered for unused REs (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For used REs, all spatial streams are always used. [End CB012115-HA1]

Noise power per subcell is reported to L2-PS via L1-BB in field *noisePower of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespCellPs (see [11517087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVMPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Unit is dBm and granularity of the reported value is 0.1 dBm.\*\*

Noise power computation is described in section 2.7.3.1 of "5GMax algorithm specification".

---

#### 7.4.6.5.2 Noise power computation (measurement K1)

##### 7.4.6.5.2.1 Thor

###### 7.4.6.5.2.1.0-3 Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor 11413702: Thor L1-SW computes noise power based on 1st DMRS symbol, it provides averaged noise power per antenna (spatial stream) and normalized to one RE (see 5G_L1_13595_replaced( 11493778 )). L1-SW shall normalize this noise power to one PRB: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1_{norm,a}(u) = N_{RB}^{SC} \times \hat{\sigma} a^2(u)$. The equation consists of the following elements: - A constant 'K' multiplied by a subscripted '1' which is also subscripted with 'norm,a'. This entire term is a function of 'u'. - An equals sign '='. - A term denoted as '$N {RB}^{SC}$', which appears to be a variable with superscripts. - A multiplication symbol 'x'. - A term denoted as '$\hat{\sigma} a^2(u)$', which represents a variable with a hat, a subscript 'a', a superscript '2', and is also a function of 'u'.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2422.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] where u represents the grant index, from 1 to Ngrants, [CB010708-G-UPD002] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor scomp to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming. scomp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored.  Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor scomp [End CB010708-G-UPD002] Then, noise power shall be aggregated over receiving antennas (spatial streams) allocated to the UE: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1 {norm}(u) = \sum_{a=1}^{nRx} K1_{norm,a}(u)$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2422.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] where nRx represents the number of receiving antennas. The noise power per sub-cell is then averaged over grants: [image-2][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1_{cell} = \frac{\sum_{u=1}^{N_{grants}} K1_{norm}(u)}{N_{grants}}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2422.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] Noise power is converted to dBm, with application of the scaling factor. The formula is given in 5G_L1_8903_replaced( 11421828 ) for Thor L1 HW, The minimum value of noise power is -140 dBm: - if K1&lt;-140 dBm then K1=-140 dBm (ID: 11413702)

##### 7.4.6.5.2.2 Odin

###### 7.4.6.5.2.2.0-1 Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin 12657268: Odin L1-SW computes noise power based on 1st DMRS symbol, it provides averaged noise power per antenna (spatial stream) and normalized to one RE (see 5G_L1_13595_replaced( 11493778 )). L1-SW shall normalize this noise power to one PRB: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1_{norm,a}(u) = N_{RB}^{SC} \times \hat{\sigma} a^2(u)$. The equation consists of the following elements: - A constant 'K' multiplied by a subscripted '1' which is also subscripted with 'norm,a'. This entire term is a function of 'u'. - An equals sign '='. - A term denoted as '$N {RB}^{SC}$', which appears to be a variable with superscripts. - A multiplication symbol 'x'. - A term denoted as '$\hat{\sigma}_a^2(u)$', which represents a variable with a hat, a subscript 'a', a superscript '2', and is also a function of 'u'.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2421.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] where u represents the grant index, from 1 to N grants, [CB012115-HA1] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor s comp to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming. s comp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored.  Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor s comp **[End CB012115-HA1] * Then, noise power shall be aggregated over receiving antennas (spatial streams) allocated to the UE: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1_{norm}(u) = \sum_{a=1}^{nRx} K1_{norm,a}(u)$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2421.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] where nRx represents the number of receiving antennas. The noise power per sub-cell is then averaged over grants: [image-2][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $K1_{cell} = \frac{\sum_{u=1}^{N_{grants}} K1_{norm}(u)}{N_{grants}}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_2421.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] Noise power is converted to dBm, with application of the scaling factor. The formula is given in 11421828 for Odin L1 HW, The minimum value of noise power is -140 dBm: - if K1&lt;-140 dBm then *K1=-140 dBm (ID: 12657268)

#### 7.4.6.5.3 Received Interference and Thermal Noise Power per PRB

##### 7.4.6.5.3.1 Thor

**7.4.6.5.3.1.0-3**  (ID: `11413745`)

11413745:

11413745:
Thor
Noise per PRB

[CB010708-G-UPD002] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor scomp to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming. scomp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor scomp [End CB010708-G-UPD002]

PRB-wise noise power is averaged over all received antennas (spatial streams) [CB010708-G-UPD002] after compensation [End CB010708-G-UPD002] and over layers as follows:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
noisePower(prb) = $\frac{N\_{SC}^{RB}}{N\_{RX}N\_{Layer}} \frac{\sum\_{ant=1}^{N\_{Rx}} \sum\_{p=1}^{N\_{Layer}} \hat{\sigma}*{noise,prb,p,ant}^2}{2^{t*{Agc}}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2426.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where tAgc is the post-FFT scaling factor.

If MU-MIMO is enabled and multiple UEs are sharing the same PRB, PRB-wise noise is averaged over UEs:

L1-RU shall report PRB-wise noise power to L1-BB in logarithmic scale in dBm unit, using array noisePerPrb in message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespCellPs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14996\_replaced([11517087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVMPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in 5G\_L1\_17386\_replaced([11422764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-i65vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If measurement is invalid (all received I/Q data are filled with zeros), PRB-wise noise power shall be set to -140 dBm.

**Noise per PRB**

[CB012115-HA1] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor *s*comp *to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming.* s*comp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor* s*comp* *[End CB012115-HA1]****\****\*

PRB-wise noise power is averaged over all received antennas (spatial streams) [CB012115-HA1] after compensation [End CB012115-HA1] and over layers as follows:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
noisePower(prb) = $\frac{N\_{SC}^{RB}}{N\_{RX}N\_{Layer}} \sum\_{ant=1}^{N\_{Rx}} \sum\_{p=1}^{N\_{Layer}} \hat{\sigma}\_{noise,prb,p,ant}^2$ / $2^{tAgc}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2425.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where tAgc is the post-FFT scaling factor.

If MU-MIMO is enabled and multiple UEs are sharing the same PRB, PRB-wise noise is averaged over UEs:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
noisePower(prb) = $\frac{\frac{N\_{SC}^{RB}}{N\_{RX}N\_{u}N\_{Layer}} \sum\_{ant=1}^{N\_{RX}} \sum\_{u=1}^{N\_{u}} \sum\_{p=1}^{N\_{Layer}} \hat{\sigma}\_{noise,prb,u,p,ant}^2}{2^{tAgc}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2425.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

L1-RU shall report PRB-wise noise power to L1-BB in logarithmic scale in dBm unit, using array *noisePerPrb in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespCellPs (see [11517087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVMPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in [11422764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-i65vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).\*\*

If measurement is invalid (all received I/Q data are filled with zeros), PRB-wise noise power shall be set to -140 dBm.
