#### 7.4.6.5.4 Noise power per antenna

##### 7.4.6.5.4.1 Thor

**7.4.6.5.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11413757`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall also compute noise power per antenna (spatial stream) and per grant K1norm,a(u) (see 5G\_L1\_15378\_replaced([11413648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-BWevvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in linear scale.

[CB010708-G-UPD002] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor scomp to compensate the measurement K1norm,a(u) in case of split-panel beamforming. scomp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor scomp [End CB010708-G-UPD002]

Noise power per antenna shall be reported to L1-BB in field linNoiseOfAnt of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14999\_replaced([11517105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8M_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Unit is attoWatt (1 aW = 10-18 W) with 1 aW precision.

Linear scaling factor shall be applied, as specified in: 5G\_L1\_17163\_replaced([11422966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-i66fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor-RU.

In case of a fake UE (see 5G\_L1\_17154\_replaced([11412293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e96BtvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the reported noise value for each antenna shall be set equal to the RSSI value (see 5G\_L1\_8319\_replaced([11404480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9UL0PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), with 32-bit saturation.

---

##### 7.4.6.5.4.2 Odin

**7.4.6.5.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `12657367`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall also compute noise power per antenna (spatial stream) and per grant *K1*norm,a*(u) (see [11413648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-BWevvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in linear scale.*\*\*

[CB012115-HA1] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor *s*comp *to compensate the measurement* K1*norm,a*(u) in case of split-panel beamforming. *s*comp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor *s*comp. [End CB012115-HA1]***\****\*\*\*

Noise power per antenna shall be reported to L1-BB in field *linNoiseOfAnt of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see [11517105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8M_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Unit is attoWatt (1 aW = 10-18 W) with 1 aW precision.\*\*

Linear scaling factor shall be applied, as specified in: [11422966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-i66fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for Odin-RU.

In case of a fake UE (see [11412293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e96BtvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the reported noise value for each antenna shall be set equal to the RSSI value (see [11404480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9UL0PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with 32-bit saturation.

---

### 7.4.6.6 Signal to Interference &amp; Noise Ratio (SINR)

#### 7.4.6.6.1 Post Combiner SU SINR (PUSCH MU receiver only)

##### 7.4.6.6.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.6.1.1.0-3**  (ID: `11413785`)

Thor
For Thor and MU MIMO Receiver:

For each scheduled UE on PUSCH, if it belongs to a virtual UE that has more than two paired UEs **[CB008235-C-UPD002] on at least one of the allocated PRBs** [End CB008235-C-UPD002], 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall compute one post equalized SU SINR measurement per layer. The result shall be reported to 5G-L2-PS via 5G-L1-UL (BB) in IE *suPostCombSinr of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (5G\_L1\_IF\_15102\_replaced([11517114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8NfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**\***\*

The measurement computation is described in section **#eq-PuschSuPostCombSinr** of 5gmax algorithm specifications.\*\*\*\*

Note:

1. The above functionality shall be skipped if *postSuSinr in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_14983\_replaced([11517052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is disabled (value is 0). In this case, *suPostCombSinr shall be set as invalid value (-255 dB).*\*\*
2. **[Before CB008235-C-UPD002] Only the pairing of root UE and normal UE supports post-equalized SU SINR estimation. The pairing of root UE and UE candidate group is out of the scope.** [CB008235-C-UPD002] As long as the virtual UE has at least one PRB that is shared by more than two paired UEs, the measurement needs to be conducted for all paired UEs belong to this virtual UE. **[End CB008235-C-UPD002]**\*\*\*\*
3. The number of PRBs used for post-equalized SU SINR estimation is determined by rdparameter *rdNbPrbSuSinr16Rx (5G\_L1\_16489\_replaced([11414183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-EZzPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and they are selected uniformly for each paired UE with PRBs that have central DC excluded. Only the middle 4 subcarriers of selected PRBs are used.*

[PR852695]  
4. The PRB which contains DC subcarrier shall not be used for the suPostCombSinr measurement. If UE has only 1 PRB allocation and it contains DC, suPostCombSinr shall be set to invalid value (-255 dB) . See section 2.3.6 in 5gmax algorithm specification and 5G UP Algorithm: [SU SINR for PUSCH MU receiver (post-equalized)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)  
for more info.    
[End PR852695]

---

##### 7.4.6.6.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12815463`)

Odin
For Odin and MU MIMO Receiver:

For each scheduled UE on PUSCH, if it belongs to a virtual UE that has more than two paired UEs, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall compute one post equalized SU SINR measurement per layer. The result shall be reported to 5G-L2-PS via 5G-L1-UL (BB) in IE *suPostCombSinr of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs ([11517114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8NfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

The measurement computation is described in section**[#eq-PuschSuPostCombSinr](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#eq-PuschSuPostCombSinr)**of 5gmax algorithm specifications.\*\*\*\*

Note:

1. The above functionality shall be skipped if *postSuSinr in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq ([11517052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is disabled (value is 0). In this case, *suPostCombSinr shall be set as invalid value (-255 dB).*\*\*
2. Only the pairing of root UE and normal UE supports post-equalized SU SINR estimation. The pairing of root UE and UE candidate group is out of the scope.
3. The number of PRBs used for post-equalized SU SINR estimation is determined by rdparameter *rdNbPrbSuSinr16Rx ([11414183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-EZzPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and they are selected uniformly for each paired UE with PRBs that have central DC excluded. Only the middle 4 subcarriers of selected PRBs are used.*

[CB012115-MN]  
4. The PRB which contains DC subcarrier shall not be used for the suPostCombSinr measurement. If UE has only 1 PRB allocation and it contains DC, suPostCombSinr shall be set to invalid value (-255 dB) . See section 2.3.6 in 5gmax algorithm specification and 5G UP Algorithm: [SU SINR for PUSCH MU receiver (post-equalized)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)  
for more info.    
[End CB012115-MN]

---

#### 7.4.6.6.2 Antenna-wise SINR

##### 7.4.6.6.2.1 Thor

**7.4.6.6.2.1.0-3**  (ID: `11413811`)

Thor
For Thor-RU and SU or MU-MIMO Receiver with up to [Before CB008235-A] 4 [CB008235-A] 8 [End CB008235-A] paired UEs per PRB:

For each scheduled UE on PUSCH, L1-RU shall compute one SINR measurement per spatial stream and NR-slot for beam management usage. Depending on the number of spatial streams,   [Before CB008235-A] 4, 8, 16 [CB008235-A] 2, 4, 8, or 16 [End CB008235-A] estimates shall be then provided to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in IE sinrOfAnt of structure fhPuschAntMeas of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.

The SINR estimation per rx antenna stream on PUSCH is described in section 2.7.5.1 of 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: although antenna-wise value is introduced for beam management purpose, antenna-wise SINR is also sent when beamforming is disabled.

---

##### 7.4.6.6.2.2 Odin

**7.4.6.6.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `12657370`)

Odin
For Odin-RU and SU [CB012115-HA1] or MU [End CB012115-HA1] MIMO Receiver [CB012115-HA1] with up to 4 paired UEs per PRB [End CB012115-HA1]:

For each scheduled UE on PUSCH, L1-RU shall compute one SINR measurement per spatial stream and NR-slot for beam management usage. Depending on the number of spatial streams, 8 or 16 estimates shall be then provided to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in IE *sinrOfAnt of structure* fhPuschAntMeas of message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.*\*\*

The SINR estimation per rx antenna stream on PUSCH is described in section [#sec-MeasSinrPusch](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-MeasSinrPusch) of 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: although antenna-wise value is introduced for beam management purpose, antenna-wise SINR is also sent when beamforming is disabled.

---

#### 7.4.6.6.3 Antenna-wise measurement mapping

**7.4.6.6.3.1.0-4**  (ID: `11413843`)

Thor
Antenna-wise measurements described in above sections are sent in a dynamic array of structures *fhPuschAntMeas in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15103\_replaced([11517124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8N_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Measurements of each spatial stream are placed in one of these structures. The mapping of spatial streams to beam pattern ID is shown in the table below.\*\*

| C16’2, C16’4, **[CB008235-A]** C16'8 **[End CB008235-A]** | **puschAntMeas[0]** | patternId[0] | stream 0 | CB010708-A |
| **puschAntMeas[1]** | patternId[0] | stream 1 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[2]** | patternId[1] | stream 2 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[3]** | patternId[1] | stream 3 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[4]** | patternId[2] | stream 4 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[5]** | patternId[2] | stream 5 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[6]** | patternId[3] | stream 6 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[7]** | patternId[3] | stream 7 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[8]** | patternId[4] | stream 8 | CB010708-C |  |
| **puschAntMeas[9]** | patternId[4] | stream 9 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[10]** | patternId[5] | stream 10 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[11]** | patternId[5] | stream 11 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[12]** | patternId[6] | stream 12 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[13]** | patternId[6] | stream 13 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[14]** | patternId[7] | stream 14 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[15]** | patternId[7] | stream 15 |  |  |

**[End CB008235-SR-X]**

In case of SU-MIMO grant, the size of **puschAntMeas is given by *ueReceiverSize (*ueReceiverSize in PuschReceiveReqGrant structure of UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15101\_replaced([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), that is,* *puschAntMeas[0]...**puschAntMeas[*ueReceiverSize-1] are the only valid addressing indices for antenna-wise measurements.*****\***\*

In case of MU receiver, structure **fhPuschAntMeas is delivered for all beams. Measurements for UE own beams are located in** fhPuschAntMeas[startAntIdx] to **fhPuschAntMeas[startAntIdx+2*numOfBeams-1] where numOfBeams is the number of valid patternId received by current UE.***\*\*\*

---

##### 7.4.6.6.3.2 Odin

**7.4.6.6.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `12657377`)

Odin
Antenna-wise measurements described in above sections are sent in a dynamic array of structures *fhPuschAntMeas in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15103\_replaced([11517124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8N_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Measurements of each spatial stream are placed in one of these structures. The mapping of spatial streams to beam pattern ID is shown in the table below.\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | Measurements for antenna i | Beam ID | spatial stream | First feature |
| C16’2, C16’4 | **puschAntMeas[0]** | patternId[0] | stream 0 | CB012115-SR-HA |
| **puschAntMeas[1]** | patternId[0] | stream 1 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[2]** | patternId[1] | stream 2 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[3]** | patternId[1] | stream 3 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[4]** | patternId[2] | stream 4 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[5]** | patternId[2] | stream 5 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[6]** | patternId[3] | stream 6 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[7]** | patternId[3] | stream 7 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[8]** | patternId[4] | stream 8 | CB012115-SR-HA |  |
| **puschAntMeas[9]** | patternId[4] | stream 9 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[10]** | patternId[5] | stream 10 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[11]** | patternId[5] | stream 11 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[12]** | patternId[6] | stream 12 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[13]** | patternId[6] | stream 13 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[14]** | patternId[7] | stream 14 |  |  |
| **puschAntMeas[15]** | patternId[7] | stream 15 |  |  |

In case of SU-MIMO grant, the size of **puschAntMeas is given by *ueReceiverSize (*ueReceiverSize in PuschReceiveReqGrant structure of UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq, [11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), that is,* *puschAntMeas[0]...**puschAntMeas[*ueReceiverSize-1] are the only valid addressing indices for antenna-wise measurements.*****\***\*

[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, structure **fhPuschAntMeas is delivered for all beams. The measurements for UE own beams are located in** fhPuschAntMeas[startAntIdx] to **fhPuschAntMeas[startAntIdx+2*numOfBeams-1] where numOfBeams is the number of valid patternId received by current UE. [End CB012115-HA1]***\*\*\*

---

### 7.4.6.7 Received Signal Strength Indicator (RSSI)

#### 7.4.6.7.1 RSSI report

**7.4.6.7.1.0-2**  (ID: `12657379`)

RSSI report
L1-RU shall estimate one RSSI on PUSCH per slot and per UE, combined over all receiving spatial streams. It shall report it to L1-BB within the field *rssi sent in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs message. This information is then forwarded to L2-PS for long term (LT) averaging.\*\*

The RSSI estimation algorithm on PUSCH is described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

~~When only zero-valued samples are got from all the receiving antennas (e.g. broken antenna scenario), L1-RU shall set the~~ ~~rssi~~~~IE in~~ ~~UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs~~ ~~message to INVALID value (-140 dBm).~~

[CB012115-SR-HA]The requirement is valid for Odin.[End CB012115-SR-HA]

---

#### 7.4.6.7.2 RSSI computation (measurement M1)

##### 7.4.6.7.2.1 Thor

**7.4.6.7.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11413906`)

Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
11413906:
Thor
L1-SW computes RSSI per antenna based on 1st DMRS pilot for each grant u. RSSI is averaged over layers and normalized to one PRB.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$M1\_{norm,a}(u) = \frac{N\_{RB}^{SC}}{N\_{layer}} \sum\_{l=0}^{N\_{layer}-1} \left( \frac{1}{N\_{pilot}^{PUSCH}} \sum\_{k=0}^{N\_{pilot}^{PUSCH}-1} (\hat{H}*{l,k,sep}^{pilot,a})^\* \cdot \hat{H}*{l,k,sep}^{pilot,a} \right)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2448.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB010708-G-UPD002] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor scomp to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming. scomp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor scomp [End CB010708-G-UPD002]

De-boosting is applied to RSSI in order to compensate frequency domain multiplexing of DMRS:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M1\_{deboost,a}(u) = \frac{(M1\_{norm,a}(u) - K \cdot 1\_{norm,a}(u))}{S\_{DMRSBoost, PUSCH}^2} + K \cdot 1\_{norm,a}(u)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2448.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

where:

* K1norm,a(u) is the noise power estimator for antenna a and user u as described in 5G\_L1\_4743\_replaced([11404108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9SWovvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* SDMRSBoost,PUSCH is the power boost factor for PUSCH DMRS (see 5GMax Algoithm Specification § 2.7.2.1).

RSSI per user is aggregated over antennas as follows:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M1\_{deboost}(u) = \sum\_{a=0}^{N\_{RX}-1} M1\_{deboost,a}(u)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2448.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

The rssi parameter are defined in dBm unit as illustrated in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Formulas for conversion to dBm unit and application of the scaling factor are given in 5G\_L1\_8903\_replaced([11421828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFvfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor.

---

##### 7.4.6.7.2.2 Odin

**7.4.6.7.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `12657382`)

Odin
12657382:

12657382:
Odin
L1-SW computes RSSI per antenna based on 1st DMRS pilot for each grant *u. RSSI is averaged over layers and normalized to one PRB.*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$M1\_{norm,a}(u) = \frac{N\_{RB}^{SC}}{N\_{layer}} \sum\_{l=0}^{N\_{layer}-1} \left( \frac{1}{N\_{pilot}^{PUSCH}} \sum\_{k=0}^{N\_{pilot}^{PUSCH}-1} (\hat{H}*{l,k,sep}^{pilot,a})^\* \cdot \hat{H}*{l,k,sep}^{pilot,a} \right)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2447.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**[CB012115-HA1] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor *s*comp* to compensate the measurement in case of split-panel beamforming. *s*comp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor *s*comp \*\*[End CB012115-HA1]******\****\*

De-boosting is applied to RSSI in order to compensate frequency domain multiplexing of DMRS:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M1\_{deboost,a}(u) = \frac{(M1\_{norm,a}(u) - K1\_{norm,a}(u))}{S\_{DMRSBoost,PUSCH}^2} + K1\_{norm,a}(u)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2447.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

where:

* *K1*norm,a(*u) is the noise power estimator for antenna* a and user *u as described in [11404108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9SWovvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*\*\*\*\*
* *S*DMRSBoost,PUSCH *is the power boost factor for PUSCH DMRS (see section [#sec-MeasRssiPusch](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-MeasRssiPusch) of 5GMax Algorithm Specification).*\*\*

RSSI per user is aggregated over antennas as follows:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$M1\_{deboost}(u) = \sum\_{a=0}^{N\_{RX}-1} M1\_{deboost,a}(u)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_2447.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

The *rssi parameter are defined in dBm unit as illustrated in [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

Formulas for conversion to dBm unit and application of the scaling factor are given in [12582290](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NxbeEjRXEfCKaNlcHOQWmg) for Odin.

---

#### 7.4.6.7.3 RSSI per antenna

**7.4.6.7.3.0-2**  (ID: `12815475`)

RSSI per antenna
5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall estimate RSSI on PUSCH per slot, per UE and per antenna (spatial stream), normalized to 1 PRB *M1*deboost,a*(u), as defined in [11413868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-CkmPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*\*\*

**[CB012115-HA1] For each spatial stream, apply the scaling factor *s*comp* to compensate the measurement  *M1*deboost,a*(u) in case of split-panel beamforming.* s*comp is 1 for full panel beamforming case and therefore it can be ignored. Refer to section §5.3.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification for the definition of scaling factor* s*comp* \*[End CB012115-HA1]******\****\*\*\*\*

It shall report this RSSI measurement in linear scale, in field *linRssiOfAnt of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see [11517105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8M_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Unit is attoWatt (1 aW = 10-18 W) with precision of 1 aW.\*\*

Formula for application of the linear scaling factor is specified in [11422966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-i66fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

In case of a fake UE (flag *fakeUe is set to TRUE in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRes), as no real signal is supposed to be received, RSSI measurement shall be considered as noise and interference measurement.\*\*

The requirement is supported in Thor. [CB012115-HA] It shall also be supported in Odin. [End CB012115-HA]

---

### 7.4.6.8 Discontinuous Transmission (DTX) - Partial Detection

#### 7.4.6.8.1 DTX Metric

##### 7.4.6.8.1.1 Thor

**7.4.6.8.1.1.0-3**  (ID: `11413946`)

Thor
Partial DTX for 1 and 2 PRB allocation in L1-RU

L1-RU shall compute the PUSCH DTX metric according to the algorithm described by equation [PDF tag eq-PuschIfftDtxDetMetricPrb12] in the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Partial DTX status shall be reported to L1-BB in IE dtx of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.

L1-RU shall report DTX metric value to L1-BB in IE dtxMetric of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L1-RU shall report DTX threshold value to L1-BB in IE dtxThreshold of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Final DTX detection will be done in L1-BB after decoding, see 5G\_L1\_14241\_replaced([11406892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9fyB_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

See also 5G\_L1\_19483\_replaced([11407107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9hAJPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 7.4.6.8.1.2 Odin

**7.4.6.8.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12677205`)

Odin
Partial DTX detection status

L1-RU shall compute the PUSCH DTX metric according to the algorithm described in section 2.3.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The IFFT based method shall be used to derive the DTX metric.

L1-RU shall report DTX metric value to L1-BB in IE dtxMetric of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: The false alarm target for this metric is set to 0.5% with false alarm is defined as the probability to detect data whereas nothing was sent on PUSCH.

PUSCH DTX implementation is based on "antenna-wise" approach described in section "2.3.8 PUSCH DTX Detection" of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L1-RU shall determine partial DTX detection status by comparing DTX metric to the applicable DTX threshold determined as per 5G\_L1\_14041\_replaced([11413958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-DLo_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Partial DTX status shall be reported to L1-BB in IE dtx of message UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.

---

#### 7.4.6.8.2 DTX threshold selection

##### 7.4.6.8.2.1 Thor

**7.4.6.8.2.1.0-5**  (ID: `12706831`)

Thor
(Since 26R1) 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX detection depending on the number of spatial streams, the number of layers, the number of DMRS CDM group without data, the orthogonal code coverage status and the number of allocated PRBs, as described below. This selection shall be performed for each UE scheduled on PUSCH.

1.  From *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message, L1-RU gets the two parameters* numOfLayers and *numOfPrb. Supported values for* numOfPrb are given in 5G\_L1\_13526\_replaced([11411586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-Z_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It shall then obtain the *numOfEffectivePrb as below:*\*\*\*\*

If *numOfPrb >= 43*

*numOfEffectivePrb = 43*

Else

*numOfEffectivePrb =* numOfPrb\*\*

EndIf

2.  According to parameters *numOfStreams, numOfLayers, numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData and* Occ status, 5G-L1-UL shall select proper set of PUSCH DTX thresholds as described in section “2.3.8 PUSCH DTX Detection” of "5GMAX algorithm specification".\*\*

[Before CB008235-SR-X]

• The *numOfStreams is derived according to cell type and receiver size:*

o If cell is C4'2, numOfStreams =4.

o Else

if UE is not paired, *numOfStreams =*ueReceiverSize from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.*\*\*

If UE is paired, *numOfStreams = 2x* numOfBeams, where *numOfBeams equals size of* patternId from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.*\*\*\*\*

o End

[CB008235-SR-X]

• The *numOfStreams is derived according to receiver size and UE's beam number:*

If UE is not paired, *numOfStreams =*ueReceiverSize from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.*\*\*

If UE is paired, *numOfStreams = 2x* numOfBeams, where *numOfBeams equals size of* patternId from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.*\*\*\*\*

[End CB008235-SR-X]

• *numOfLayers and* numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData are obtained from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*\*\*

• The *Occ status is derived according to* numOfLayers and *antPort parameter in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

o If *numOfLayers equals to 1, then the* Occ status is always No.\*\*

o If *numOfLayers equals to 2, then if* antPort equals to 0xA000, then the *Occ status is No, else the* Occ status is Yes.\*\*\*\*

Let's denote *PuschThresholds the array of size 43. L1-RU shall use* dtxThreshold  = *PuschThresholds [*numOfEffectivePrb - 1] to compute the DTX status.\*\*\*\*

Thresholds are hard-coded tables in 5G-L1-UL (Radio). 12 threshold tables are defined in 5G\_L1\_14307\_replaced([11413983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-DLp_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), indexed by (*numOfStreams,* numOfLayers , *Occ Status):*\*\*

* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx) for 1 layer without OCC,
* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx) for 2 layers without OCC,
* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx) for 2 layers with OCC.

The selected DTX threshold is sent to L1-BB in IE *dtxThreshold of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

This requirement is also appliable to RU subcell type C16'8.

---

##### 7.4.6.8.2.2 Odin

**7.4.6.8.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `12677214`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX detection depending on the number of spatial streams, the number of layers, the number of DMRS CDM group without data, the orthogonal code coverage status and the number of allocated PRBs, as described below. This selection shall be performed for each UE scheduled on PUSCH.

1.  From *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message, L1-RU gets the two parameters* numOfLayers and *numOfPrb. Supported values for* numOfPrb are given in 5G\_L1\_13526\_replaced([11411586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-Z_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It shall then obtain the *numOfEffectivePrb as below:*\*\*\*\*

If *numOfPrb >= 43*

*numOfEffectivePrb = 43*

Else

*numOfEffectivePrb =* numOfPrb\*\*

EndIf

2.  According to parameters *numOfStreams, numOfLayers, numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData and* Occ status, 5G-L1-UL shall select proper set of PUSCH DTX thresholds as described in section “2.3.8 PUSCH DTX Detection” of "5GMAX algorithm specification".\*\*

• The *numOfStreams is derived according to cell type and receiver size:*

o if UE is not paired, *numOfStreams =*ueReceiverSize from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq.*\*\*

o [CB012115-HA1] If UE is paired, *numOfStreams = 2x* numOfBeams, where *numOfBeams equals size of* patternId from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq. [End CB012115-HA1]*\*\*\*\*

• *numOfLayers and* numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData are obtained from *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see [11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*\*\*

• The *Occ status is derived according to* numOfLayers and *antPort parameter in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message (see [11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

o If *numOfLayers equals to 1, then the* Occ status is always No.\*\*

o If *numOfLayers equals to 2, then if* antPort equals to 0xA000, then the *Occ status is No, else the* Occ status is Yes.\*\*\*\*

Let's denote *PuschThresholds the array of size 43. L1-RU shall use* dtxThreshold  = *PuschThresholds [*numOfEffectivePrb - 1] to compute the DTX status.\*\*\*\*

Thresholds are hard-coded tables in 5G-L1-UL (Radio). 12 threshold tables are defined in [11413983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-DLp_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), indexed by (*numOfStreams,* numOfLayers , *Occ Status):*\*\*

* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx ) for 1 layer without OCC,
* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx ) for 2 layers without OCC,
* 4 tables (2Rx, 4Rx, 8Rx and 16Rx ) for 2 layers with OCC.

The selected DTX threshold is sent to L1-BB in IE *dtxThreshold of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

---

### 7.4.6.9 Rank Computation Based on DMRS

#### 7.4.6.9.1 Thor

**7.4.6.9.1.0-4**  (ID: `12743220`)

Thor
**Rank (Since 26R1)**

5G-L1-UL(RU) shall compute the UL rank, the rank metric computation is described in section 2.9 of "5GMax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_2794).

The number of subcarriers used to calculate UL rank is 6 per allocated PRB. Subcarriers used to calculate UL rank are distributed in equal distance. More details are described in section "2.9 RI Selection" of "5Gmax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_2794). The simulation report is available at “[RI selection optimization.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/RI%20selection%20optimization.pptx)”.

Per RX antenna SNR is used in RI selection.

In case of MU receiver, rank shall be computed based on antenna-wise SNR from UE own spatial streams (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The computation of the UL rank metric depends on parameter value of *spatialMode,* numOfLayers, pBoost (in case of equal to or more than 4Rx receiver is used) as described in the algorithm document. These parameters are within the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message.*\*\*

**[Before CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

For MU MIMO UEs following rules shall be applied:

for cell type C16'2, C16'4, C16'8 5G-L1-UL shall compute rank:

* using noise from all DMRS REs
* using own UE antennas or UE beams.

**[CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

For MU MIMO UEs following rules shall be applied:

1. for cell type C16'4 and C16'8 with enabled enhancement L1 noise computation algorithm (pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement==true in message CombiningLinkConf of HLAPI, refer to [11630917: CombiningLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ayugjfwmee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")) 5G-L1-UL shall compute rank:

- using noise from own DMRS REs only;  
              - using all antennas.

2. Applicable to the following two scenarios: 1) Cell types other than C16'4 and C16'8; 2) Cell types C16'4 and C16'8 with the L1 noise computation enhancement algorithm disabled (where the parameter pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement is set to false in the CombiningLinkConf message of HLAPI, refer to [11630917: CombiningLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ayugjfwmee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9") ),

5G-L1-UL shall ignore parameter pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement and shall compute rank:

- using noise from all DMRS REs  
               - using own UE antennas or UE beams.

**[End CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

The UL rank metric result also depends on threshold value in IE *ulRiSelectionThreshold of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15101\_replaced([11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

The computation of the UL rank metric is done when PUSCH is received with spatial multiplexing rank 2. The computed UL rank shall be sent to L2-PS via L1-BB in IE *ulRank of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.\*\*

For spatial multiplexing rank 1 or single antenna Tx/singleTx, the UL rank metric is not computed and the IE *ulRank is forced to INVALID value and sent to L2-PS via L1-BB in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

*ulRank IE is described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15102\_replaced([11517114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8NfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

---

#### 7.4.6.9.2 Odin

**7.4.6.9.2.0-1**  (ID: `12677408`)

Odin
**Rank**

5G-L1-UL(RU) shall compute the UL rank, the rank metric computation is described in section [#sec-RiSelectRiSel](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-RiSelectRiSel) of The 5GMax Algorithm Specification (see 5G\_L1\_2794). The simulation report is available at [RI selection optimization.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/RI%20selection%20optimization.pptx?d=we9ddf4f12f1e46ef877ec229615dcac2&csf=1&web=1&e=nhyaGT).

The number of subcarriers used to calculate UL rank is 6 per allocated PRB. Subcarriers used to calculate UL rank are distributed in equal distance. More details are described in section "2.9 RI Selection" of "5Gmax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_2794). The simulation report is available at “[RI selection optimization.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/RI%20selection%20optimization.pptx)”.

Per RX antenna SNR is used in Rank Indication (RI) selection.

[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, rank shall be computed based on antenna-wise SNR from UE own spatial streams (see [11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB012115-HA1]

The computation of the UL rank metric depends on parameter value of *spatialMode,* numOfLayer, *pBoost (in case of more than 4Rx receiver is used) as described in the algorithm document. These parameters are within the* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message.\*\*\*\*

The UL rank metric result also depends on threshold value in IE *ulRiSelectionThreshold of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq (see [11517061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVK_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

The computation of the UL rank metric is done when PUSCH is received with spatial multiplexing rank 2. The computed UL rank shall be sent to L2-PS via L1-BB in IE *ulRank of message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs.\*\*

For spatial multiplexing rank 1 or single antenna Tx/singleTx, the UL rank metric is not computed and the IE *ulRank is forced to INVALID value and sent to L2-PS via L1-BB in message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs (see [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

*ulRank IE is described in [11513848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlA_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

---

### 7.4.6.10 Transmission Precoding Matrix Indicator (TPMI) Selection based on DMRS

#### 7.4.6.10.1 Thor

**7.4.6.10.1.0-4**  (ID: `12590044`)

Thor
**TPMI selection (Since 26R1)**

TPMI selection is described in section "2.9 PMI Selection"of "5GMax algorithm specification" (see 5G\_L1\_2794).

The computation of the TPMI is done when PUSCH is received with spatial multiplexing rank 2 (*numOfLayers =2 in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq). The computed TPMIs and corresponding SINR values shall be sent to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14998\_replaced([11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):*\*\*

- *ulRank (see 5G\_L1\_13663\_replaced([11414124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-EZw_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*

- *ulPmiRank1 is the result of MECG metric. Supported values are [0..5].*

- *ulPmiRank1Sinr is the SINR for given* ulPmiRank1 expressed in dB. If the computed value is larger than 40dB, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall cap it to 40dB**.**\*\*

- *ulPmiRank2 is the result of SLP metric. Supported values are [0..2]. The simulation report is available at “[NR\_UplinkPMISelection.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/NR_UplinkPMISelection.pptx)”.*

- *ulPmiRank2Sinr*is the SINR for given *ulPmiRank2 expressed in dB. If the computed value is larger than 40dB, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall cap it to 40dB**.*\*\*\*\*

The number of equidistant subcarriers considered for PMI evaluation on PUSCH is 12.

The codebook used for the computation of the metrics depends on parameter value of *spatialMode,* numOfLayer, pboost (in case of equal to or more than 4Rx receiver is used) **and *codebookIndex as described in the algorithm document. These parameters come within the \*UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14982\_replaced([11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\*\*\*

Also, the codebook used for the computation of the metrics depend on *puschTransCoherence IE that comes within the* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message: the codebooks for cases "*puschTransCoherence ==* nonCoherent" and "*puschTransCoherence ==* fullCoherent" are given in 5G\_L1\_13639\_replaced([11411972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e94zkfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\***\*

In case of MU receiver, TPMI computation shall be base on the spatial stream allocated to the UE (see 5G\_L1\_15228\_replaced([11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[Before CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

For MU MIMO UEs following rules shall be applied:

1. for cell type C16'2, C16'4, C16'8 5G-L1-UL shall compute TPMI:

- using noise from all DMRS REs

- using own UE antennas or UE beams.

**[CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

For MU MIMO UEs following rules shall be applied:

1. for cell type C16'4 and C16'8 with enabled enhancement L1 noise computation algorithm (pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement==true in message CombiningLinkConf of HLAPI, refer to [11630917: CombiningLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ayugjfwmee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")) 5G-L1-UL shall compute TPMI:

- using noise from own DMRS REs only;  
              - using all antennas.

2. Applicable to the following two scenarios: 1) Cell types other than C16'4 and C16'8; 2) Cell types C16'4 and C16'8 with the L1 noise computation enhancement algorithm disabled (where the parameter pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement is set to false in the CombiningLinkConf message of HLAPI, refer to [11630917: CombiningLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYugJfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ayugjfwmee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9") ),

5G-L1-UL shall ignore parameter pmi\_sinr\_ul\_mu\_mimo\_enhancement and shall compute TPMI:

- using noise from all DMRS REs  
               - using own UE antennas or UE beams.

**[End CB008235-SR-D-UPD002]**

For spatial multiplexing rank 1 (*numOfLayers =1 in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq), the UL TPMI selection metrics are not computed and the following parameters are set to INVALID value (255) in the message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs:*\*\*

- *ulRank,*

- *ulPmiRank1,*

*- ulPmiRank2*

In that case, also corresponding SINR values are not meaningful:

- *ulPmiRank1Sinr and*

- *ulPmiRank2Sinr*

Note: In rank 1 SRS channel is used instead and resulting metrics are reported in message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_14953\_replaced([11517282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKKWfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

For spatial mode single antenna (singleTx), the UL TPMI selection metrics are not computed and the parameter *ulPmiRank1 and ulPmiRank2 are set to INVALID value and sent to 5G-L2-PS vla L1-BB in the message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs. Values of *ulPmiRank1Sinr and* ulPmiRank2Sinr are also not meaningful in that case.\*\*\*\*

---

#### 7.4.6.10.2 Odin

**7.4.6.10.2.0-1**  (ID: `12677414`)

Odin
**TPMI selection**

TPMI selection is described in section [#sec-PmiSelect](https://sv-ul-5gmax.dyn.nesc.nokia.net/AlgoSpec/main.pdf#sec-PmiSelect) of the 5GMax Algorithm Specification (see 5G\_L1\_2794).

The computation of the TPMI is done when PUSCH is received with spatial multiplexing rank 2 (*numOfLayers =2 in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq). The computed TPMIs and corresponding SINR values shall be sent to 5G-L2-PS via L1-BB in the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs message (see [11517101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSI8MvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):*\*\*

- *ulRank (see [11414124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-EZw_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

- *ulPmiRank1 is the result of MECG metric. Supported values are [0..5].*

- *ulPmiRank1Sinr is the SINR for given* ulPmiRank1 expressed in dB. If the computed value is larger than 40dB, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall cap it to 40dB**.**\*\*

- *ulPmiRank2 is the result of SLP metric. Supported values are [0..2]. The simulation report is available at [NR\_UplinkPMISelection.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/NR_UplinkPMISelection.pptx?d=w25f46d72d5f44263abb50210dab55ac4&csf=1&web=1&e=bx9gP8).*

- *ulPmiRank2Sinr*is the SINR for given *ulPmiRank2 expressed in dB. If the computed value is larger than 40dB, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall cap it to 40dB**.*\*\*\*\*

The number of equidistant subcarriers considered for PMI evaluation on PUSCH is 12.

The codebook used for the computation of the metrics depends on parameter value of *spatialMode,* numOfLayer, *pboost (in case of more than 4Rx receiver is used)* *and* codebookIndex as described in the algorithm document. These parameters come within the *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message described in [11517049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVKPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).***\***\*

Also, the codebook used for the computation of the metrics depend on *puschTransCoherence IE that comes within the* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq message: the codebooks for cases "*puschTransCoherence ==* nonCoherent" and "*puschTransCoherence ==* fullCoherent" are given in [11411972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e94zkfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**\***\*

**[CB012115-HA1] In case of MU receiver, TPMI computation shall be base on the spatial stream allocated to the UE (see [11411631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e92-bfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CB012115-HA1]\*\*\*\*

For spatial multiplexing rank 1 (*numOfLayers =1 in* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveReq), the UL TPMI selection metrics are not computed and the following parameters are set to INVALID value (255) in the message *UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs:*\*\*

- *ulRank,*

- *ulPmiRank1,*

*- ulPmiRank2*

In that case, also corresponding SINR values are not meaningful:

- *ulPmiRank1Sinr and*

- *ulPmiRank2Sinr*

Note: In rank 1 SRS channel is used instead and resulting metrics are reported in message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs ([11517282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKKWfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

For spatial mode single antenna (singleTx), the UL TPMI selection metrics are not computed and the parameter *ulPmiRank1 and ulPmiRank2 are set to INVALID value and sent to 5G-L2-PS vla L1-BB in the message* UlDataFH\_PuschReceiveRespUePs. Values of *ulPmiRank1Sinr and* ulPmiRank2Sinr are also not meaningful in that case.\*\*\*\*

## 7.4.7 R&amp;D Parameters

### 7.4.7.1 Post-equalized SU SINR Estimation

**7.4.7.1.0-3**  (ID: `12815509`)

Post-equalized SU SINR Estimation
*rdNbPrbSuSinr16Rx*

This parameter indicates number of PRBs used for post equalized SU SINR estimation in case of MU receiver

Value range: 1. 18 (max value to be refined after benchmarks)

Default value:**18**

Unit: -

Online modifiable: Yes

Step size: 1

Specified in [11413767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-B9hvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

Trigger for deletion: never

Note: This parameter is applied on Thor RU. Refer to [11110503](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpE7BfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

The parameter is applicable to Thor [CB012115-HA1] and Odin. [End CB012115-HA1]

---

### 7.4.7.2 Mixture PDP Method

**7.4.7.2.0-1**  (ID: `11414206`)

Mixture PDP Method
This parameter indicates if mixture PDP method is enabled for all UEs of all subcells in the same RU.

Value range: 0 (disabled), 1(enabled)

Default value: 1(enabled)

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_L1\_18576\_replaced([11412929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e99sEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: never

Note: This parameter is applied on Thor RU. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28108\_replaced([11110534](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpFiCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 7.4.7.3 DMRS Type 2 Threshold

**7.4.7.3.0-1**  (ID: `11414217`)

DMRS Type 2 Threshold
rdDmrsPowerType2ThrPusch

Value range: 0(0.00)...1000(1.000)

Default value: 10(0.010)

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step size: 1(0.001)

Specified in 5G\_L1\_17580\_replaced([11412794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e98d-PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

## 7.4.8 PUSCH Capacity

### 7.4.8.1 Number of Scheduled UEs

#### 7.4.8.1.1 Thor

##### 7.4.8.1.1.0-3 Thor Placeholder; proper requirement for Thor RU, if needed Refer to 5G_L1_15199_replaced( 11409412 ) (Thor BB) (ID: 11414258)

#### 7.4.8.1.2 Odin

**7.4.8.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12677417`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL(radio) shall support the scheduling of multiple UEs in a single slot within the cell.

The maximal number of scheduled UEs per cell per slot: 9.

The maximal number of scheduled UEs per Odin per slot: 36

Note:

L1 RU capacity per Odin is limited by maximal number of carriers (CC) equals 4 and maximal occupied bandwidth (oBW) equals 200 MHz.

For details of subcells deployment please see 5G\_UP\_2513 (“nrCellType definition” chapter in 5G UP System module).

For details of mapping between the subcell in the L1-BB and in the L1-RU please refer to 5G\_UP\_10480.

For estimation (within CB012115-SR-HA) feasibility of commercial capacity targets 5G-L1-UL(radio) shall support the scheduling up to 16 UEs in a single slot within the cell.

Conformance Testing

2) G-FR1-A9-2
